Dingoo Tech A330 >> Dingoo

Show Register

main.c 

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <dingoo/slcd.h>
#include <dingoo/cache.h>
#include <dingoo/keyboard.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdbool.h>
#include <stdint.h>
#include <dingoo/ucos2.h>
#include <dingoo/entry.h>
#include <sml/graphics.h>
#include <sml/display.h>
#include <sml/control.h>
#include <sml/timer.h>

#include "FontWhite.h"

#define CONTROL_BUTTON_SELECT 0x00000400

unsigned short *g_pGameDecodeBuf = 0L;

void PutChar(int X, int Y, unsigned char Char)
{
  int x, y;
  unsigned short *frame = _lcd_get_frame();

  for(y=0; y<CHAR_HEIGHT; y++){
    for(x=0; x<CHAR_WIDTH; x++){
      frame[(Y * CHAR_HEIGHT + y) * 320 + (X * CHAR_WIDTH + x)] = CHARS[Char][y * CHAR_WIDTH + x];
    }
  }
}

void PutString(int X, int Y, char *Str)
{
  while(*Str != 0) {
    PutChar(X, Y, *Str);
    X++;
    Str++;
    if(X > 39){
      X = 0;
      Y++;
      if(Y > 13){
        Y = 0;
      }
    }
  }
}

int main(int argc, char** argv)
{
  unsigned long b[30]={0};

  __asm__ __volatile__ (
    "sw $v0, %[a0]  \n"
    "sw $v1, %[a1]  \n"
    "sw $a0, %[a2]  \n"
    "sw $a1, %[a3]  \n"
    "sw $a2, %[a4]  \n"
    "sw $a3, %[a5]  \n"
    "sw $t0, %[a6]  \n"
    "sw $t1, %[a7]  \n"
    "sw $t2, %[a8]  \n"
    "sw $t3, %[a9]  \n"
    "sw $t4, %[a10]  \n"
    "sw $t5, %[a11]  \n"
    "sw $t6, %[a12]  \n"
    "sw $t7, %[a13]  \n"
    "sw $s0, %[a14]  \n"
    "sw $s1, %[a15]  \n"
    "sw $s2, %[a16]  \n"
    "sw $s3, %[a17]  \n"
    "sw $s4, %[a18]  \n"
    "sw $s5, %[a19]  \n"
    "sw $s6, %[a20]  \n"
    "sw $s7, %[a21]  \n"
    "sw $t8, %[a22]  \n"
    "sw $t9, %[a23]  \n"
    "sw $k0, %[a24]  \n"
    "sw $k1, %[a25]  \n"
    "sw $gp, %[a26]  \n"
    "sw $sp, %[a27]  \n"
    "sw $fp, %[a28]  \n"
    "sw $ra, %[a29]  \n"
    :
    [a0] "=m" (b[0]), [a1] "=m" (b[1]), [a2] "=m" (b[2]), [a3] "=m" (b[3]), [a4] "=m" (b[4]), [a5] "=m" (b[5]),
    [a6] "=m" (b[6]), [a7] "=m" (b[7]), [a8] "=m" (b[8]), [a9] "=m" (b[9]), [a10] "=m" (b[10]), [a11] "=m" (b[11]),
    [a12] "=m" (b[12]), [a13] "=m" (b[13]), [a14] "=m" (b[14]), [a15] "=m" (b[15]), [a16] "=m" (b[16]), [a17] "=m" (b[17]),
    [a18] "=m" (b[18]), [a19] "=m" (b[19]), [a20] "=m" (b[20]), [a21] "=m" (b[21]), [a22] "=m" (b[22]), [a23] "=m" (b[23]),
    [a24] "=m" (b[24]), [a25] "=m" (b[25]), [a26] "=m" (b[26]), [a27] "=m" (b[27]), [a28] "=m" (b[28]), [a29] "=m" (b[29])
    :
    :"memory"
  );

  char buf[32]={0};
  char *reg[] = { 
    "$v0", "$v1", "$a0", "$a1", "$a2", "$a3",
    "$t0", "$t1", "$t2", "$t3", "$t4", "$t5", "$t6", "$t7",
    "$s0", "$s1", "$s2", "$s3", "$s4", "$s5", "$s6", "$s7",
    "$t8", "$t9", "$k0", "$k1", "$gp", "$sp", "$fp", "$ra"
  };

  unsigned int x, y, idx=0;
  for(y=0; y<10; y++){
    for(x=0; x<3; x++){
      sprintf(buf, "%s:%08x", reg[idx], b[idx]);
      idx+= 1;
      PutString(x*13, y, buf);
    }
  }

  KEY_STATUS KS;
  __dcache_writeback_all();
  _lcd_set_frame();
  do {
    _kbd_get_status(&KS);
  }while((KS.status & CONTROL_BUTTON_SELECT) == 0);
  return EXIT_SUCCESS;
}

Makefile 

APP_NAME  = show_reg
CPP       = mipsel-linux-g++
CC        = mipsel-linux-gcc
LD        = mipsel-linux-ld
SOURCE    = .
INCLUDE   = -I$(DINGOO_SDK)/include -I../lib -I$(MIPSTOOLS)/mipsel-linux/include -I$
W_OPTS    = -Wall -Wextra -finline-functions -fomit-frame-pointer -msoft-float -fno-builtin -fno-exceptions
CPP_OPTS  = -G0 -O3 $(INCLUDE) -mips32 -mno-abicalls -fno-pic $(W_OPTS) -D_DEBUG -DMPU_JZ4740 -c
CC_OPTS   = -G0 -O3 $(INCLUDE) -mips32 -mno-abicalls -fno-pic $(W_OPTS) -D_DEBUG -DMPU_JZ4740 -c
CC_OPTS_A = $(CC_OPTS) -D_ASSEMBLER_

LIB_PATH  = $(DINGOO_SDK)/lib
LIBS      = -lc -ljz4740 -lgcc

LD_SCRIPT = $(DINGOO_SDK)/lib/dingoo.xn
LD_OPTS   = -nodefaultlibs --script $(LD_SCRIPT) -L$(LIB_PATH) $(LIBS) -o $(APP_NAME).elf

SRC_CPP = $(foreach dir, $(SOURCE), $(wildcard $(dir)/*.cpp))
SRC_C   = $(foreach dir, $(SOURCE), $(wildcard $(dir)/*.c))
SRC_S   = $(foreach dir, $(SOURCE), $(wildcard $(dir)/*.S))
OBJ_CPP = $(patsubst %.cpp, %.o, $(SRC_CPP))
OBJ_C   = $(patsubst %.c, %.o, $(SRC_C))
OBJ_S   = $(patsubst %.S, %.o, $(SRC_S))
OBJ     = $(OBJ_CPP) $(OBJ_C) $(OBJ_S)

.PHONY : all
all : $(APP_NAME).app

$(APP_NAME).app : $(APP_NAME).elf
	$(DINGOO_SDK)/tools/elf2app/elf2app $(APP_NAME)

$(APP_NAME).elf : $(OBJ)
	$(LD) $(OBJ) $(LD_OPTS)

$(OBJ_CPP) : %.o : %.cpp
	$(CPP) $(CPP_OPTS) -o $@ $<

$(OBJ_C) : %.o : %.c
	$(CC) $(CC_OPTS) -o $@ $<

$(OBJ_S) : %.o : %.S
	$(CC) $(CC_OPTS_A) -o $@ $<

.PHONY : clean
clean :
	rm -f $(OBJ) $(APP_NAME).elf $(APP_NAME).bin $(APP_NAME).app

完成
